Welles Wilder, calculates price movement using speed and changes as its measuring points. This momentum indicator compares the scope of latest gains to latest losses in an attempt to determine overbought and oversold assets based on the closing prices of a recent trading period.</li>\n<li><strong>Moving Average</strong> â The Moving Average is a widely used indicator that calculates information and analyzes data points by creating a series of averages. These averages are calculated using a number of subsets taken from a complete set of data. The Moving Average is used to indicate the direction of the current trend and helps provide clean data by removing daily price fluctuations found in the financial data.</li>\n<li><strong>âBollinger Bandsâ</strong> â Is based on a technical analysis tool invented by John Bollinger, it uses a simple moving average and two standard deviations. There is middle band, one upper band and one lower band. The algorithm creates a moving channel of prices composed of an over sell channel and over bought channel. The algorithm then compares the last executed price in the channel and creates a sell or a buy signal.</li>\n</ul>\n<p>Once the trader has chosen one of the three strategies, the Strategy Advisor Calculator will calculate the data and will provide a call / put recommendation based on previous expiries of the asset.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>This is a revolutionary device that will help make a prediction based on the real trends of an asset.  'value': newVal,\n            'min': 0,\n            'max': 100,\n            'font': '\"Dosis\", sans-serif',\n            'inputColor': '#000000',\n            \"readOnly\": true,\n            \"thickness\": .33,\n            'dynamicDraw': true,\n            \"displayInput\": true,\n            'format': function(value) {\n                return value + '%';\n            }\n        });\n\n        // animate knob\n        $({\n            value: 0\n        }).animate({\n            value: newVal\n        }, {\n            duration: 1000,\n            easing: 'swing',\n            progress: function() {\n                knobElement.val(Math.ceil(this.value)).trigger('change');\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    function doKnobTest(knobElement) {\n        //console.log('doKnobTest: changing knob...');\n        setTimeout(function() {\n            doKnobChange(knobElement, 33.33);\n        }, 1500);\n        setTimeout(function() {\n            doKnobChange(knobElement, 66.66);\n         }, 3000);\n    }\n\n    function doFileValidation(fileInput, fileRemoveBtn, fileUploadBtn) {\n        var filename = fileInput.val().split('\\\\').pop();\n        var filenameExt = fileInput.val().split('.').pop().toLowerCase();\n\n        // check strings\n        if (filename === '' || filenameExt === '') {\n            //console.log('doFileValidation: error during file validation (empty)');\n            // disable buttons\n            fileRemoveBtn.prop('disabled', true);\n            fileUploadBtn.prop('disabled', true);\n            //console.log(fileUploadBtn.prop('disabled'));\n            return false;\n            // check extension\n        } else if ($.inArray(filenameExt, ['gif', 'png', 'jpg', 'jpeg', 'pdf', 'doc', 'docx']) == -1) {\n            //console.log('doFileValidation: error during file validation (invalid extension)');\n            // enable buttons\n            fileRemoveBtn.prop('disabled', true);\n            fileUploadBtn.prop('disabled', true);\n            //console.log(fileUploadBtn.prop('disabled'));\n            return false;\n            // then pass successfuly\n        } else {\n            //console.log('doFileValidation: file validation successful...');\n            // enable buttons\n            fileRemoveBtn.prop('disabled', false);\n            fileUploadBtn.prop('disabled', false);\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    function doFileUpload(fileInput, fileUploadBtn, knobElement, statusIcon) {\n        //console.log('doFileUpload: uploading file...');\n        fileUploadBtn.addClass('loading');\n        var data = new FormData();\n        data.append('file_upload', true);\n        data.append('file', $('input[name=' + fileInput.attr('name') + ']')[0].files[0]);\n        var uploadAction = $.ajax({\n            url: \"https://www.binaryuno.com/wp-content/themes/BinaryUno/includes/file-upload.php\",\n            type: 'POST',\n            data: data,\n            cache: false,\n            contentType: false,\n            processData: false,\n            xhr: function() {\n                var myXhr = $.ajaxSettings.xhr();\n                return myXhr;\n            }\n        });\n        uploadAction.done(function(msg) {\n            // upload done\n            //console.log('doFileUpload: upload successful');\n            fileUploadBtn.removeClass('loading');\n            fileUploadBtn.prop('disabled', true);\n\n            // update status icon for section\n            if (statusIcon.attr('class') == 'bu-icon nok') {\n                statusIcon.removeClass('nok').addClass('ok');\n            }\n            // update knob status\n            if (!knobElement) {\n                var knobElement = $('.status-knob');\n            }\n            var percentsCompleted = $('.bu-icon.ok').length * 33.3333;\n            doKnobChange(knobElement, percentsCompleted);\n        });\n\n        uploadAction.fail(function(jqXHR, textStatus) {\n            // if upload failed\n            //console.log('doFileUpload: upload failed!');\n            fileUploadBtn.removeClass('loading');\n        });\n    }\n\n    function initFileSelect(fileInput, fileNameInput, fileChooseBtn, fileRemoveBtn, fileUploadBtn) {\n        // on Click\n        fileChooseBtn.click(function() {\n            //console.log('initFileSelect: selecting file...');\n            fileInput.trigger('click');\n        });\n\n        // on Change\n        fileInput.change(function() {\n            // not sure about this line\n            // var fileInput = $(this);\n            //console.log('initFileSelect: file selected, checking file...');\n            if (doFileValidation(fileInput, fileRemoveBtn, fileUploadBtn) == true) {\n                // validation is ok -> pass filename\n                //console.log('initFileSelect: validation passed, initializing file field...');\n                var filename = fileInput.val().split('\\\\').pop();\n                fileNameInput.val(filename);\n            } else {\n                // raise error\n                //console.log('initFileSelect: validation not passed, error');\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    function initFileRemove(fileRemoveBtn, uploadRow) {\n        // on click\n        fileRemoveBtn.click(function() {\n            //console.log('initFileRemove: resetting elements...');\n            // resetting inputs\n            uploadRow.children('input').each(function() {\n                $(this).after($(this).val('').clone()).remove();\n            });\n            // resetting buttons\n            uploadRow.children('button, a').each(function() {\n                $(this).after($(this).clone()).remove();\n            });\n            //console.log('initFileRemove: reinitializing row scripts...');\n            // reinitializing row scripts\n            initUploadRow(uploadRow);\n        });\n    }\n\n    function initFileUpload(fileInput, fileUploadBtn, knobElement, statusIcon) {\n        // on click\n        fileUploadBtn.click(function() {\n            // launch upload action\n            //console.log('initFileUpload: launching upload...');\n            doFileUpload(fileInput, fileUploadBtn, knobElement, statusIcon);\n        });\n    }\n\n    function initRowAdd(uploadRow, rowAddBtn) {\n        // upload row template\n        var uploadRowHtml = '<div class=\"row-upload\">' +\n            '<input type=\"file\" name=\"file1\" class=\"hidden upload_unput\" accept=\"image/*,.doc,.pdf,.docx\">' +\n            '<input class=\"file_name\" readonly>' +\n            '<button type=\"button\" class=\"narrow_button choose_file\"><span>Choose File</span></button>' +\n            '<button type=\"button\" class=\"narrow_button upload_file\"><span>Upload File</span></button>' +\n            '<button type=\"button\" class=\"narrow_button remove_file\"><span>Remove File</span></button>' +\n            '<a href=\"javascript:void(0);\" class=\"add_upload_row\">Add row</a>' +\n            '<a href=\"javascript:void(0);\" class=\"remove_upload_row\">Remove row</a>' +\n            '</div>';\n\n        //on Click\n        rowAddBtn.click(function() {\n            var totalUploadRows = rowAddBtn.parent().siblings('.row-upload').length + 1;\n\n            // max 3 fields\n\n            if (totalUploadRows < 3) {\n                // adding row...\n                //console.log('initRowAdd: adding new row...');\n                uploadRow.after(uploadRowHtml);\n                initUploadRow(uploadRow.next());\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    function initRowRemove(uploadRow, rowRemoveBtn) {\n        //on Click\n        rowRemoveBtn.click(function() {\n            var totalUploadRows = rowRemoveBtn.parent().siblings('.row-upload').length + 1;\n            // min 1 fields\n            if (totalUploadRows > 1) {\n                // removing row...\n                //console.log('initRowAdd: adding new row...');\n                uploadRow.remove();\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    function initUploadRow(uploadRow, knobElement) {\n        var statusIcon = uploadRow.parents('li').first().children('.bu-acc-label').children('.bu-icon:first'),\n            fileInput = uploadRow.children('input:file'),\n            fileNameInput = uploadRow.children('.file_name'),\n            fileChooseBtn = uploadRow.children('.choose_file'),\n            fileRemoveBtn = uploadRow.children('.remove_file').prop('disabled', true),\n            fileUploadBtn = uploadRow.children('.upload_file').prop('disabled', true),\n            rowAddBtn = uploadRow.children('.add_upload_row'),\n            rowRemoveBtn = uploadRow.children('.remove_upload_row');\n        // init elements\n        //console.log('initUploadRow: initializing row elements...');\n        initFileSelect(fileInput, fileNameInput, fileChooseBtn, fileRemoveBtn, fileUploadBtn);\n        initFileRemove(fileRemoveBtn, uploadRow);\n        initFileUpload(fileInput, fileUploadBtn, knobElement, statusIcon);\n        initRowAdd(uploadRow, rowAddBtn);\n        initRowRemove(uploadRow, rowRemoveBtn);\n    }\n\n    function initUploadForm(uploadForm, uploadRowHtml) {\n        var accordion = uploadForm.find('.bu-acc'),\n            knobElement = uploadForm.find('.status-knob');\n        //console.log('initUploadForm: initializing accordion...');\n        //accordion.jsAccordion();\n        //console.log('initUploadForm: accordion ready, initializing knob...');\n        //doKnobChange(knobElement, 0);\n        //doKnobTest(knobElement);\n        //console.log('initUploadForm: knob ready, initializing first \"upload row\"...');\n        $(\".row-upload\").each(function() {\n            initUploadRow($(this), knobElement);\n        });\n        //console.log('initUploadForm: \"upload row\" ready...');\n    }\n\n    function initUploadModalButton() {\n        var uploadForm = $('#file-uploads');\n        var uploadModalButton = $('.open-files-modal');\n        //console.log('initUploadModalButton: initializing upload modal button...');\n        //console.log(uploadForm.length);\n        // if one upload form exists\n        if (uploadForm.length > 0) {\n            // initialize upload form\n            initUploadForm(uploadForm);\n            // on Click\n            uploadModalButton.click(function() {\n                var uploadTab = $('#upload');\n                if (uploadTab) {\n                    // activate uload form tab\n                    uploadTab.trigger('click');\n                }\n                // scroll to existing form\n                $(\"html, body\").animate({scrollTop: 200}, \"slow\");\n                //console.log('initUploadModalButton: scrolling to existing upload form...');\n                return false;\n            });\n            // if there are no upload forms\n        } else if (uploadForm.length === 0) {\n            // on Click\n            uploadModalButton.on('click', function() {\n                // create modal with upload form\n                doCreateUploadsModal();\n            });\n        }\n    }\n    $(initUploadModalButton);\n})(jQuery);\n</script>\n\n<div id=\"SnapABug_W\"
